AASB	O
9	O
Financial	O
Instruments	O
This	O
standard	O
is	O
applicable	O
to	O
annual	O
reporting	O
periods	O
beginning	O
on	O
or	O
after	O
1	O
January	O
2018.	O
The	O
standard	O
replaces	O
all	O
previous	O
versions	O
of	O
AASB	O
9	O
and	O
completes	O
the	O
project	O
to	O
replace	O
IAS	O
39	O
“	O
Financial	O
Instruments	O
:	O
Recognition	O
and	O
Measurement	O
”	O
.	O

AASB	O
9	O
introduces	O
new	O
classification	O
and	O
measurement	O
models	O
for	O
financial	O
assets.	O
A	O
financial	O
asset	O
shall	O
be	O
measured	O
at	O
amortised	O
cost	O
,	O
if	O
it	O
is	O
held	O
within	O
a	O
business	O
model	O
whose	O
objective	O
is	O
to	O
hold	O
assets	O
in	O
order	O
to	O
collect	O
contractual	O
cash	O
flows	O
,	O
which	O
arise	O
on	O
specified	O
dates	O
and	O
solely	O
principal	O
and	O
interest.	O
All	O
other	O
financial	O
instrument	O
assets	O
are	O
to	O
be	O
classified	O
and	O
measured	O
at	O
fair	O
value	O
through	O
profit	O
or	O
loss	O
unless	O
the	O
entity	O
makes	O
an	O
irrevocable	O
election	O
on	O
initial	O
recognition	O
to	O
present	O
gains	O
and	O
losses	O
on	O
equity	O
instruments	O
(	O
that	O
are	O
not	O
held-for-trading	O
)	O
in	O
other	O
comprehensive	O
income	O
(	O
“	O
OCI	O
”	O
)	O
.	O

For	O
financial	O
liabilities	O
,	O
the	O
standard	O
requires	O
the	O
portion	O
of	O
the	O
change	O
in	O
fair	O
value	O
that	O
relates	O
to	O
the	O
entity	O
’	O
s	O
own	O
credit	O
risk	O
to	O
be	O
presented	O
in	O
OCI	O
(	O
unless	O
it	O
would	O
create	O
an	O
accounting	O
mismatch	O
)	O
.	O

New	O
simpler	O
hedge	O
accounting	O
requirements	O
are	O
intended	O
to	O
more	O
closely	O
align	O
the	O
accounting	O
treatment	O
with	O
the	O
risk	O
management	O
activities	O
of	O
the	O
entity.	O
New	O
impairment	O
requirements	O
will	O
use	O
an	O
‘	O
expected	O
credit	O
loss	O
’	O
(	O
“	O
ECL	O
”	O
)	O
model	O
to	O
recognise	O
an	O
allowance.	O
Impairment	O
will	O
be	O
measured	O
under	O
a	O
12-month	O
ECL	O
method	O
unless	O
the	O
credit	O
risk	O
on	O
a	O
financial	O
instrument	O
has	O
increased	O
significantly	O
since	O
initial	O
recognition	O
in	O
which	O
case	O
the	O
lifetime	O
ECL	O
method	O
is	O
adopted.	O
The	O
standard	O
introduces	O
additional	O
new	O
disclosures.	O
The	O
Group	O
does	O
not	O
expect	O
any	O
material	O
impact	O
from	O
the	O
ultimate	O
adoption	O
of	O
AASB	O
9.	O
AASB	O
16	O
Leases	O
This	O
standard	O
is	O
applicable	O
to	O
annual	O
reporting	O
periods	O
beginning	O
on	O
or	O
after	O
1	O
January	O
2019.	O
The	O
standard	O
replaces	O
AASB	O
117	O
”	O
Leases	O
”	O
and	O
for	O
lessees	O
will	O

of	O

and	O

Subject	O

,	O

”	O

”	O

of	O

,	O

”	O

”	O

or	O

as	O

A	O

will	O

,	O

for	O
lease	O
prepayments	O
,	O
lease	O
incentives	O
received	O
,	O
initial	O
direct	O
costs	O
incurred	O
and	O
an	O
estimate	O
of	O
any	O
